<h3>Premium Hosting at Premium Prices</h3>
<a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=255164&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937719&post_id=255164&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=vendor&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="255164" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC img-link" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937719', 'kinsta', this,  true, ReturnPopup  );"><figure id="attachment_3138048" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3138048"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:61.8125% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--1.png"  width="1600" height="989" alt="Kinsta WordPress Hosting" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--1.png"   width="1600" height="989" alt="Kinsta WordPress Hosting" class="border wp-image-3138048 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3138048"class="wp-caption-text">Kinsta offers outstanding WordPress hosting, for a price</figcaption></figure></a>
<p><strong>Kinsta does a lot to differentiate itself from other hosting providers.</strong> Instead of operating its own servers, it provides managed hosting on Google’s enterprise-level network. While it only provides managed WordPress hosting for websites, it also offers application and database hosting.</p>
<p>And while Kinsta doesn’t come bundled with a bunch of optional add-ons like typical shared hosts, I appreciated its focus on features that give you more control and a better hosting experience.</p>
<p>It’s also, to put it lightly, <i>not cheap</i>. Mind you, it’s not outrageously expensive for what it offers.</p>
<p>I wanted to know if Kinsta was worth its price or if you’d be better off going with a cheaper host and treating yourself to a nice dinner with the leftover money. That’s why<strong> I put in over two weeks of careful testing and research into Kinsta.</strong> The verdict? Though it’s not the cheapest option out there, <strong>Kinsta’s fully managed WordPress hosting is absolutely worth it.</strong></p>
<p>It’s an ideal choice if you’re running a small-to-medium business, or want to provide your web development clients with high-end hosting, or even if you have loftier ambitions for your personal site. However, it might be overkill for smaller passion projects.</p>
<p>Kinsta’s service is available in Danish, Dutch, English, French, German, Italian, Japanese, Portuguese, Spanish, and Swedish. Is it what <i>you</i> need to take your website to the next level? Read on to find out.</p>

id="features">Features</span></h2>

<div class="section-content content"></span></p>
<h3>Laser-Focused on Top-Performance Hosting, Without the Classic Extras</h3>
<p><strong>There are a lot of popular features offered by other hosting providers that Kinsta simply doesn’t have.</strong> There’s no proprietary website builder, search engine optimization (SEO) analysis, or significant marketing tools. It doesn’t even offer domain name registration, free or otherwise. Does that mean that Kinsta’s offering is limited? Not exactly – it’s just more <i>focused.</i></p>
<p>Instead of bloating its service with a bunch of nice-to-have add-ons that you’d be better off getting through a third-party service anyway, <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=255164&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937707&post_id=255164&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=vendor&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="255164" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937707', 'kinsta', this,  true, ReturnPopup  );">Kinsta’s features are dedicated to giving you the best performance</a> possible.</p>
<h3><div id="true">True Managed WordPress Hosting</div></h3>
<p>When Kinsta advertises managed WordPress hosting, it really does mean <i>managed</i>. Immediately after sign-up, <strong>Kinsta takes care of the entire WordPress installation for you</strong>. From there, you can activate or deactivate any installed plugins and themes, manage multiple WordPress sites at once, and tinker with your site’s settings, all from your dashboard.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3138077" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3138077"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:46% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--2.png"  width="1600" height="736" alt="Kinsta Edge Caching" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--2.png"   width="1600" height="736" alt="Kinsta Edge Caching" class="border wp-image-3138077 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3138077"class="wp-caption-text">Kinsta offers a wide variety of useful features for WordPress management</figcaption></figure>
<p>If you worry about security, Kinsta comes with state-of-the-art firewalls and DDoS protection. You also get access to customizable security rules like banning certain IP addresses. To mitigate a worst-case scenario, it autosaves daily backups of your site to prevent losing important data. If all else fails, <strong>Kinsta even promises to fix your site for you.</strong></p>
<p>I also liked the option to activate edge and mobile caching. Edge caching duplicates your site’s assets on more than 260 data centers around the world. To improve performance, it uses the copies stored nearest to each site visitor. You can also choose to create cached versions of your site specifically for mobile to improve your loading speeds on those devices.</p>
<p>Though it doesn’t offer domain registration, Kinsta comes with its own domain name system (DNS) that allows you to manage all your domain settings directly. It also provides you with a limited number of free SSL certificates.</p>
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=255164&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937708&post_id=255164&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=vendor&amp=0" data-id="255164" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937708', 'kinsta', this,  true, ReturnPopup  );">Discover More Kinsta Features &gt;&gt;</a></div>
<h3>Plenty of Monitoring Tools To Assess the State of Your Site</h3>
<p>Performance and usage analytics are crucial for optimizing your website, and <strong>Kinsta offers two different performance monitoring tools and advanced usage analytics.</strong></p>
<p>If you want to track your website’s performance and identify bottlenecks, you can access the application performance monitoring (APM) and New Relic monitoring (NRM) tools directly from your hosting dashboard. APM is a proprietary tool that captures time-stamped information about your site’s PHP processes. NRM gives you performance information by adding custom JavaScript to your site&#8217;s front end.</p>
<p>While my team and I prefer to do all performance tests through our trusted third-party monitoring tools, <strong>these features can be useful for fine-tuning your site performance</strong>. You can also access detailed usage analytics under the Analytics tab on your dashboard.</p>
<h3>Premium Add-Ons for Impressive Performance Speeds</h3>
<p>For an extra fee, <strong>Kinsta offers a wide range of impressive <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=255164&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937709&post_id=255164&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=vendor&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="255164" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937709', 'kinsta', this,  true, ReturnPopup  );">performance-enhancing add-ons</a></strong><strong>.</strong> You can access Redis technology to improve your database read speeds or use NGINX to load WordPress from a subdirectory while your site files load from the main directory.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3138106" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3138106"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:52.8125% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--3.png"  width="1600" height="845" alt="Kinsta Premium Add-ons" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--3.png"   width="1600" height="845" alt="Kinsta Premium Add-ons" class="border wp-image-3138106 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3138106"class="wp-caption-text">Kinsta offers great additional features if you’re willing to pay for them</figcaption></figure>
<p>For extra peace of mind, you can also pay a small fee to store external backups of your site on Amazon’s or Google’s cloud storage centers.</p>
<h3>Specialized Plans for Application and Database Hosting</h3>
<p>Though managed WordPress hosting is the focus of this review, I’d be remiss not to mention Kinsta’s specialized application and database hosting plans. Application hosting offers unlimited, concurrent builds on a single account. You&#8217;ll also get scalable resources and access to Kinsta’s proprietary API.</p>
<p>For databases, Kinsta offers support for MySQL, PostgreSQL, Maria DB, and Redis, as well as automatic daily backups and up to 5 manual backups per day.</p>

<div class="section-content content"></span></p>
<h3>Fantastic Overall Ease of Use, With Some Room for Improvement</h3>
<p>Kinsta does everything in its power to ensure that setting up and running your website is as easy and fast as it can be. I can’t argue with the results. <strong>Kinsta offers <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=255164&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937710&post_id=255164&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=vendor&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="255164" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937710', 'kinsta', this,  true, ReturnPopup  );">one of the smoothest hosting experiences</a></strong><strong> I’ve had with any provider.</strong></p>
<p>Since it doesn’t offer domain name registration, I’ll admit I was a little frustrated trying to point my domain name to Kinsta’s servers. While it does offer a full DNS service, it&#8217;s odd that such a we’ll-do-it-for-you service doesn’t have one of the most basic web hosting features. But even then, most of my troubles came from my own confusion. You can’t blame Kinsta too much for that.</p>
<h3>Creating a New Account with Kinsta</h3>
<p><strong>Creating your Kinsta account could not be more straightforward.</strong> All you have to do is go to Kinsta’s homepage, select the plan that sounds best to you, and click <i>choose.</i></p>
<p>After that, you’ll have to input your billing information and select any add-ons you want (you can also add these later). Then, you’ll have to choose a name for your site and select your data center location. Once your payment goes through – it took less than a minute for me – you’ll be the proud owner of a ready-to-use Kinsta account.</p>
<h3>Connecting a Domain Name and Installing WordPress</h3>
<p>As soon as you finish creating your account, you’ll get your first taste of the Kinsta dashboard. From there, all you’ll have to do is click on the <i>create site </i>button under the <i>WordPress Site </i>option. <strong>If you already have .zip files for plugins and themes, you don’t even need to go to your WordPress dashboard to add them.</strong> You can do it directly from the Kinsta dashboard.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3138135" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3138135"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:42% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--4.png"  width="1600" height="672" alt="Kinsta Create a WordPress Site" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--4.png"   width="1600" height="672" alt="Kinsta Create a WordPress Site" class="border wp-image-3138135 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3138135"class="wp-caption-text">The Create a site button is right there – you really can’t miss it</figcaption></figure>
<p><strong>The process of connecting my domain name was a little more involved.</strong> I had to start by changing the nameservers to point to Kinsta’s servers. Once a “nameservers point to Kinsta” message appeared, I went to the Domains tab on my dashboard and clicked on <i>Add a Domain</i>. Then… nothing happened.</p>
<p>Even though my domain was pointing to Kinsta, Kinsta didn’t recognize it as a valid address for my WordPress site. I spent a good while trying to figure out how to fix this problem, until I realized I needed to add an “A” DNS record from Kinsta.</p>
<p>Though that’s a rookie mistake, <strong>I was a bit annoyed that Kinsta didn’t provide enough instruction to help me identify my problem, let alone solve it</strong>.</p>
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=255164&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937711&post_id=255164&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=vendor&amp=0" data-id="255164" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937711', 'kinsta', this,  true, ReturnPopup  );">Get Started With Kinsta &gt;&gt;</a></div>
<h3>Kinsta Offers a CDN Straight Out of the Box</h3>
<p>If you want to reach a global audience, you’ll need a content delivery network (CDN) to avoid very long load times in parts of the world that are far away from your server. <strong>Many hosts make you connect a CDN as a separate service – but not Kinsta</strong>.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3138164" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3138164"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:64.125% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--5.png"  width="1600" height="1026" alt="Kinsta CDN locations" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--5.png"   width="1600" height="1026" alt="Kinsta CDN locations" class="border wp-image-3138164 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3138164"class="wp-caption-text">Kinsta saves you the trouble of connecting your website to a CDN</figcaption></figure>
<p>To my delight, <strong>the enterprise version of Cloudflare CDN comes pre-installed on all your WordPress sites.</strong> This saves you the trouble of manually connecting to a CDN, but more importantly, it improves your global loading speeds away from your chosen data center (<a href="#per" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'per', this,  );">more on that below</a>).</p>
<h3>Easy-Access Tools To Improve Your Hosting Experience</h3>
<p>You can access a variety of useful features for managing your WordPress site directly from the <i>Tools </i>tab on your dashboard. There, you’ll be able to clear your cache, debug your site, change PHP versions, and more. The best part is that <strong>none of this requires complicated installs, as you can <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=255164&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937712&post_id=255164&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=vendor&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="255164" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937712', 'kinsta', this,  true, ReturnPopup  );">activate or deactivate any of Kinsta’s tools with the click of a button</a></strong><strong>.</strong></p>
<h3>Deploy WordPress Sites Locally With DevKinsta</h3>
<p><strong>DevKinsta provides a downloadable environment for stress-free WordPress site development.</strong> This might not seem impressive compared to the rest of Kinsta’s premium offerings, but unless you’re only migrating your site, being able to design and develop your WordPress site locally can be a huge timesaver. Once you’re satisfied with the result, DevKinsta integrates seamlessly with the Kinsta staging environment to make your site live whenever you wish.</p>

<h2 class="section-title section-title-perfomance"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" viewBox="0 0 512 512" aria-label="perfomance" role="img"><path d="m437.00002,113c-48.4,-48.4 -112.6,-75 -181,-75s-132.7,26.6 -181,75c-48.4,48.4 -75,112.6 -75,181c0,65.4 24.7,127.6 69.4,175.3l4.4,4.7l364.3,0l4.4,-4.7c44.8,-47.6 69.4,-109.9 69.4,-175.3c0.1,-68.4 -26.5,-132.7 -74.9,-181l0,0zm-12,331l-338,0c-6.8,-7.7 -13.1,-15.8 -18.8,-24.3l33.4,-19.3l-15,-26l-33.4,19.3c-13,-26.3 -20.7,-55.1 -22.7,-84.8l38.5,0l0,-30l-38.5,0c2,-30.2 10,-58.9 22.7,-84.7l33.3,19.2l15,-26l-33.3,-19.2c16.4,-24.5 37.5,-45.6 62,-62l19.2,33.3l26,-15l-19.2,-33.3c25.9,-12.8 54.5,-20.7 84.7,-22.7l0,38.5l30,0l0,-38.5c30.2,2 58.9,10 84.7,22.7l-19.2,33.3l26,15l19.2,-33.3c24.5,16.4 45.6,37.5 62,62l-33.3,19.2l15,26l33.3,-19.2c12.8,25.9 20.7,54.5 22.7,84.7l-38.3,0l0,30l38.5,0c-2,29.7 -9.7,58.5 -22.7,84.8l-33.4,-19.3l-15,26l33.4,19.3c-5.7,8.5 -11.9,16.6 -18.8,24.3l0,0z"/><path d="m272.20002,290.3l0,-94l-30,0l0,94c-19.8,6.4 -34.3,25 -34.3,46.9c0,27.2 22.1,49.3 49.3,49.3s49.3,-22.1 49.3,-49.3c0,-21.9 -14.5,-40.5 -34.3,-46.9zm-15,66.2c-10.6,0 -19.3,-8.6 -19.3,-19.3s8.6,-19.3 19.3,-19.3c10.6,0 19.3,8.6 19.3,19.3s-8.7,19.3 -19.3,19.3z"/></svg><span id="perfomance">Performance</span></h2>
</div>
<div class="section-content content">
<h3><div id="per">Kinsta Delivers Impeccable Performance</div></h3>
<p>Kinsta has more than 30 data centers across the world, meaning you’ll be able to find a location near your target audience wherever they are. Not that it matters much – <strong>due to its built-in CDN, <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=255164&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937713&post_id=255164&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=vendor&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="255164" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937713', 'kinsta', this,  true, ReturnPopup  );">Kinsta promises fast loading speeds</a></strong><strong> just about anywhere.</strong></p>
<p>To test if Kinsta was really worth all that, our team built a full landing page. This included HD images, scrolling effects, and just about everything you’d expect from a modern site. Then, we hosted it using Kinsta’s base plan and ran continuous tests for a little over two weeks. If you’re interested, you can read a full breakdown of <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/web-hosting-server-performance-tests/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">our testing methodology for hosting providers</a>.</p>
<p>The short answer: Kinsta is designed to give you the best performance and reliability it can offer. And boy-oh-boy does it deliver.</p>
<div class="hightlight-paragraph hightlight-paragraph-purple"><strong>What I found: </strong>There’s no arguing over Kinsta’s results. Over two weeks of testing, Kinsta delivered perfect uptime. Typical fully-loaded times were about 0.9s, with outstanding worldwide loading speeds.</div>
<h3>GTmetrix</h3>
<p>To test the local performance of our site, we set hourly tests for two weeks using GTMetrix with a source center near our site’s data center in Columbus. <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=255164&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937714&post_id=255164&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=vendor&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="255164" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_255164_vendor_255164_937714', 'kinsta', this,  true, ReturnPopup  );">The results were excellent across the board</a><strong>.</strong> Our site achieved a typical loading speed of about 0.9s. Even the slowest results were better than most, clocking in at about 1.4s.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3138193" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3138193"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:41.25% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--6.png"  width="1600" height="660" alt="Kinsta GTMetrix History" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--6.png"   width="1600" height="660" alt="Kinsta GTMetrix History" class="border wp-image-3138193 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3138193"class="wp-caption-text">Kinsta delivered consistently impressive loading speeds throughout the testing process</figcaption></figure>
<p>To give our readers the most accurate representation of what they will get when signing up, we tinker with the site as little as possible when testing the performance of a hosting plan. Kinsta was no exception.</p>
<p>That said, I should mention that <strong>the first time I ran Kinsta through GTMetrix, it achieved a Performance score of 100%</strong>. It would appear this was because Kinsta had automatically installed the Yoast SEO plugin on my site, which disabled my test site’s scrolling effects.</p>
<p>After deactivating the plugin, our site’s typical loading speeds saw very little loss in performance. <strong>Even without all the optimization plugins at our disposal, Kinsta’s P</strong><strong>erformance scores were regularly above 95%.</strong></p>
<figure id="attachment_3138222" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3138222"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:60.8125% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--7.png"  width="1600" height="973" alt="Kinsta Performance Score" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--7.png"   width="1600" height="973" alt="Kinsta Performance Score" class="border wp-image-3138222 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3138222"class="wp-caption-text">Kinsta consistently got “A” grades throughout testing process</figcaption></figure>
<h3>Sucuri Load Time Tester</h3>
<p>We use Sucuri’s Load Time Tester tool to test a provider’s global performance score. Now, most shared hosting providers can integrate with the free version of Cloudflare’s CDN service. That said, the signup and configuration process can be a bit of a headache. And since Cloudflare is usually a 3rd-party service, we don’t use it with our test sites. It’s what’s fair, but it does mean that even the best providers tend to struggle with global performance.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3138251" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3138251"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:69.928710304601% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--8.png"  width="1543" height="1079" alt="Kinsta Sucuri Load Time Tester Results" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--8.png"   width="1543" height="1079" alt="Kinsta Sucuri Load Time Tester Results" class="border wp-image-3138251 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3138251"class="wp-caption-text">Kinsta’s global performance was impressive</figcaption></figure>
<p>Each one of Kinsta’s WordPress plans are connected to the Enterprise level of Cloudflare’s CDN. This means that I didn’t have to do anything to maximize the site’s global performance. And <strong>the results were outstanding all over the world.</strong></p>
<h3>UptimeRobot</h3>
<p>On its service agreement, Kinsta offers a 99.9% uptime guarantee. To test if it lived up to its promises, we ran our site through over two weeks of continuous monitoring using UptimeRobot. <strong>The result was an impeccable uptime of 100%.</strong> Which doesn’t leave all that much more to say, really.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3138280" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3138280"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:39.8125% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--9.png"  width="1600" height="637" alt="Kinsta UptimeRobot Results" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--9.png"   width="1600" height="637" alt="Kinsta UptimeRobot Results" class="border wp-image-3138280 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3138280"class="wp-caption-text">You can’t ask for better uptime than 100%</figcaption></figure>
</div>
</section>

<h2 class="section-title section-title-support"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" viewBox="0 0 28 28" aria-label="support" role="img"><path d="m14,28.00001c-7.7,0 -14,-6.3 -14,-14s6.3,-14 14,-14s14,6.3 14,14s-6.3,14 -14,14zm0,-26c-6.6,0 -12,5.4 -12,12s5.4,12 12,12s12,-5.4 12,-12s-5.4,-12 -12,-12zm0,20.8c-4.9,0 -8.8,-3.9 -8.8,-8.8s3.9,-8.8 8.8,-8.8s8.8,3.9 8.8,8.8s-3.9,8.8 -8.8,8.8zm0,-15.6c-3.7,0 -6.8,3.1 -6.8,6.8s3.1,6.8 6.8,6.8s6.8,-3.1 6.8,-6.8s-3.1,-6.8 -6.8,-6.8z"/><path d="m19.5,9.50001c-0.3,0 -0.5,-0.1 -0.7,-0.3c-0.4,-0.4 -0.4,-1 0,-1.4l3.7,-3.7c0.4,-0.4 1,-0.4 1.4,0s0.4,1 0,1.4l-3.7,3.7c-0.2,0.2 -0.4,0.3 -0.7,0.3z"/><path d="m4.8,24.20001c-0.3,0 -0.5,-0.1 -0.7,-0.3c-0.4,-0.4 -0.4,-1 0,-1.4l3.7,-3.7c0.4,-0.4 1,-0.4 1.4,0s0.4,1 0,1.4l-3.7,3.7c-0.2,0.2 -0.4,0.3 -0.7,0.3z"/><path d="m23.2,24.20001c-0.3,0 -0.5,-0.1 -0.7,-0.3l-3.7,-3.7c-0.4,-0.4 -0.4,-1 0,-1.4s1,-0.4 1.4,0l3.7,3.7c0.4,0.4 0.4,1 0,1.4c-0.2,0.2 -0.5,0.3 -0.7,0.3z"/><path d="m8.5,9.50001c-0.3,0 -0.5,-0.1 -0.7,-0.3l-3.7,-3.7c-0.4,-0.4 -0.4,-1 0,-1.4s1,-0.4 1.4,0l3.7,3.7c0.4,0.4 0.4,1 0,1.4c-0.2,0.2 -0.5,0.3 -0.7,0.3z"/></svg><span id="support">Support</span></h2>
</div>
<div class="section-content content">
<h3>Good Support, but I Expected Better</h3>
<p><strong>My experience with customer support was subpar</strong>, to put it mildly. Kinsta offers live chat and email support for all paid customers, as well as phone support for sales inquiries. To test Kinsta’s support quality, I tried contacting it through every available channel. <i>Tried</i> being the operative word here.</p>
<p>The first time I sent a message through live chat, I waited for a long time without getting an answer, then missed the eventual reply – a rep’s request for my hosting address.</p>
<p>Thankfully, the second time I reached out, I received a much more prompt and comprehensive answer. However, I should point out that <strong>Kinsta&#8217;s customer support hours are misleading</strong>. While advertised as being 24/7, the actual availability is Monday to Friday from 5AM &#8211; 10PM UTC.</p>
<figure id="attachment_3138309" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3138309"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:63.4375% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--10.png"  width="1600" height="1015" alt="Kinsta Livechat Support" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/08/kinsta-review-aug-2023--10.png"   width="1600" height="1015" alt="Kinsta Livechat Support" class="border wp-image-3138309 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3138309"class="wp-caption-text">Live chat ended up being really useful, I just wished it had been on my first try</figcaption></figure>
<p>I also sent an email to test the quality of support there. No point going into too much detail because <strong>I didn’t get an answer from email support.</strong> Finally, I tried calling the sales number to ask about the e-commerce plans. My experience was much better.</p>
<p>The first thing I noticed is that since I called with a number registered in Mexico, Kinsta connected me to a Spanish-speaking support representative. They not only provided answers in my native language, but were very knowledgeable about the topics I asked about.</p>
<p>In the end, support was kind of a mixed bag. When I was able to get an answer, that answer was completely satisfactory. But <strong>I expected better</strong><strong><i>, </i></strong><strong>especially considering Kinsta’s prices</strong>.</p>
</div>
</section>

<div class="section-content content">
<h3>Kinsta Involves a Serious Investment</h3>
<p>There’s no sugar-coating it: Kinsta is quite expensive. There are 10 different plans for WordPress hosting alone. Even the entry-level plan, Starter, comes in at <span class="pricing-link"><span data-currency="USD" class="currency-symbol ">$</span><span data-currency="USD" data-price="30.00" class="currency-value">30.00</span></span> per month, or a little less if you pay annually. That’s more than the price of most other hosts’ mid-range plans, even after renewal.</p>

<h2 >FAQ<span id="FAQ"></span></h2>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Is Kinsta a good host for a WordPress site?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Yes! Kinsta offers loads of features to improve your global performance and reach. You also won’t have to worry about installing and configuring your WordPress website by yourself thanks to its outstanding <a href="#true" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'true', this,  );">fully-managed hosting</a>.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What servers does Kinsta use?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Kinsta uses enterprise-level Google Cloud servers. Thanks to its built-in CDN and wide array of global data centers, Kinsta can deliver <a href="#per" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'per', this,  );">unmatched global loading speeds</a>.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">How fast is Kinsta?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Kinsta is one of the fastest hosting providers I’ve tested. Thanks to its use of Google Cloud servers and CDN integration, performance remains excellent across the globe. If you’re interested, take a look at <a href="#per" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'per', this,  );">our in-depth Kinsta performance tests</a>.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Is Kinsta worth the price?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">That depends on your vision. Kinsta is absolutely worth its price if you have lofty ambitions for your WordPress website and you intend to reach a global audience. For smaller projects, however, you might be better off with a more affordable hosting service that doesn’t compromise on quality. 
<p></p> For basic (and cheaper) shared hosting, I recommend you check out our <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/web-hosting/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">top 10 ranking of the best hosting services in 2024</a></strong>.</span>
